## <a name="adam"></a><span data-ttu-id="e386b-693">亞當</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e386b-693">ADAM</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="e386b-694">屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e386b-694">Attributes</span></span>](#adam-attributes)

| <span data-ttu-id="e386b-1619">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e386b-1619">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e386b-1620">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e386b-1620">Value</span></span> |
